---
title: "OnShutdownRunner"
description: "Blocks until all earlier tasks have completed and then prevents further tasks from being run."
---

## OnShutdownRunner - stable

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/lifecycle/OnShutdownRunner.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait OnShutdownRunner extends HasRunOnClosing
```
